    print_header()

    show_process_info()
    print_separator()

    show_cwd()
    print_separator()

    show_memory_test()
    print_separator()

    show_bitwise_demo()
    print_separator()

    show_type_casting()
    print_separator()

    show_pointer_ops()
    print_separator()

    show_atomic_ops()
    print_separator()

    show_fork_demo()
    print_separator()

    g_sample_count = 9
    print_summary()

    print("")
    print("========================================")
    print("  All demos completed successfully!")
    print("========================================")

    return 0
}

ФАЙЛ: ./examples/bubble_sort.juno
========================================
fn main(): int {
    let arr[10]
    let size = 10

    arr[0] = 64
    arr[1] = 34
    arr[2] = 25
    arr[3] = 12
    arr[4] = 22
    arr[5] = 11
    arr[6] = 90
    arr[7] = 42
    arr[8] = 7
    arr[9] = 55

    print("Before sort:")
    for (k = 0; k < size; k++) {
        print(arr[k])
    }

    for (i = 0; i < size; i++) {
        for (j = 0; j < size - i - 1; j++) {
            let a = arr[j]
            let b = arr[j + 1]
            if (a > b) {
                arr[j] = b
                arr[j + 1] = a
            }
        }
    }

    print("After sort:")
    for (m = 0; m < size; m++) {
        print(arr[m])
    }

    return 0
}

ФАЙЛ: ./examples/gcd.juno
========================================
fn gcd(a: int, b: int): int {
    while (b != 0) {
        let temp = b
        let div = a / b
        b = a - div * b
        a = temp
    }
    return a
}

fn lcm(a: int, b: int): int {
    let g = gcd(a, b)
    return a / g * b
}

fn main(): int {
    print("=== Алгоритм Евклида ===")

    let a1 = 48
    let b1 = 18
    let g1 = gcd(a1, b1)
    print("НОД(48, 18) =")
    print(g1)

    let a2 = 56
    let b2 = 42
    let g2 = gcd(a2, b2)
    print("НОД(56, 42) =")
    print(g2)

    let a3 = 101
    let b3 = 103
    let g3 = gcd(a3, b3)
    print("НОД(101, 103) =")
    print(g3)

    print("=== НОК ===")

    let l1 = lcm(12, 18)
    print("НОК(12, 18) =")
    print(l1)

    let l2 = lcm(4, 6)
    print("НОК(4, 6) =")
    print(l2)

    return 0
}

ФАЙЛ: ./examples/benchmark.juno
========================================
fn sum_loop(n: int): int {
    let mut total = 0
    for (i = 0; i < n; i++) {
        total = total + i
    }
    return total
}

fn nested_loop(n: int): int {
    let mut count = 0
    for (i = 0; i < n; i++) {
        for (j = 0; j < n; j++) {
            count = count + 1
        }
    }
    return count
}

fn multiply_loop(n: int): int {
    let mut result = 1
    for (i = 1; i < n; i++) {
        result = result * 2
        if (result > 1000000) {
            result = 1
        }
    }
    return result
}

fn main(): int {
    prints("=== Juno Benchmark ===")

    prints("Sum 1..1000000:")
    let s = sum_loop(1000000)
    print(s)

    prints("Nested 1000x1000:")
    let n = nested_loop(1000)
    print(n)

    prints("Multiply loop 100000:")
    let m = multiply_loop(100000)
    print(m)

    prints("Math ops 1000000:")
    let mut x = 0
    for (i = 0; i < 1000000; i++) {
        x = x + i * 2 - i
    }
    print(x)

    prints("=== Done ===")
    return 0
}

ФАЙЛ: ./examples/tcp_chat_server.juno
========================================
fn main(): int {
    let server = socket(2, 1, 0)

    if (server < 0) {
        prints("Failed to create socket")
        return 1
    }

    let addr = ip(0, 0, 0, 0)
    let port = 9000

    if (bind(server, addr, port) < 0) {
        prints("Failed to bind")
        return 1
    }

    listen(server, 10)

    prints("Chat server started on port 9000")
    prints("Connect with: nc localhost 9000")

    while (1) {
        let client = accept(server)

        if (client > 0) {
            prints("Client connected!")

            let welcome = "Welcome to Juno Chat!\n"
            send(client, welcome, 21)

            let buf = getbuf()
            while (1) {
                let n = recv(client, buf, 4096)
                if (n <= 0) {
                    prints("Client disconnected")
                    break
                }

                send(client, buf, n)
            }

            close(client)
        }
    }

    close(server)
    return 0
}

import "std/thread.juno"
import "core/io.juno"

fn worker(arg) {
    let mut sum = 0
    let limit = 100000000
    let mut i = 0
    while i < limit {
        sum = (sum + i) * 3 / 3
        i = i + 1
    }
    return sum
}

fn main() {
    print_s("Juno Multithreading Benchmark Started...\n")

    let t1 = thread_spawn(worker, 1)
    let t2 = thread_spawn(worker, 2)
    let t3 = thread_spawn(worker, 3)
    let t4 = thread_spawn(worker, 4)

    thread_join(t1)
    thread_join(t2)
    thread_join(t3)
    thread_join(t4)

    print_s("Juno Benchmark Finished!\n")
    return 0
}

fn main() {
    output("\e[36m--- JUNO DEBUG CRYPT ---\e[0m");

    let name: str = "secret.txt";
    let content: str = file_read_all(name);

    if (content == "") {
        output("ERROR: Buffer is empty!");
        return 0;
    }

    output("Loaded data: ");
    output(content);

    output("Saving to output.bin...");

    let fd = file_open("output.bin", 1);
    if (fd > 0) {
        file_write(fd, content, 32);
        file_close(fd);
        output("\e[32mDONE!\e[0m");
    } else {
        output("ERROR: Cannot write!");
    }

    return 0;
}

ФАЙЛ: ./examples/crypto_tea.juno
========================================
fn tea_encrypt(v, k) {
    let mut v0 = *v
    let mut v1 = *(ptr_add(v, 1))

    let mut sum = 0
    let delta = 2654435769

    let k0 = *k
    let k1 = *(ptr_add(k, 1))
    let k2 = *(ptr_add(k, 2))
    let k3 = *(ptr_add(k, 3))

    let mut i = 0
    while (i < 32) {
        sum = (sum + delta) & 0xFFFFFFFF

        let t1 = (v1 << 4) + k0
        let t2 = v1 + sum
        let t3 = (v1 >> 5) + k1
        v0 = (v0 + (t1 ^ t2 ^ t3)) & 0xFFFFFFFF

        let t4 = (v0 << 4) + k2
        let t5 = v0 + sum
        let t6 = (v0 >> 5) + k3
        v1 = (v1 + (t4 ^ t5 ^ t6)) & 0xFFFFFFFF

        i++
    }

    *v = v0
    *(ptr_add(v, 1)) = v1
    return 0
}

fn tea_decrypt(v, k) {
    let mut v0 = *v
    let mut v1 = *(ptr_add(v, 1))

    let delta = 2654435769
    let mut sum = 3337565984

    let k0 = *k
    let k1 = *(ptr_add(k, 1))
    let k2 = *(ptr_add(k, 2))
    let k3 = *(ptr_add(k, 3))

    let mut i = 0
    while (i < 32) {
        let t4 = (v0 << 4) + k2
        let t5 = v0 + sum
        let t6 = (v0 >> 5) + k3
        v1 = (v1 - (t4 ^ t5 ^ t6)) & 0xFFFFFFFF

        let t1 = (v1 << 4) + k0
        let t2 = v1 + sum
        let t3 = (v1 >> 5) + k1
        v0 = (v0 - (t1 ^ t2 ^ t3)) & 0xFFFFFFFF

        sum = (sum - delta) & 0xFFFFFFFF
        i++
    }

    *v = v0
    *(ptr_add(v, 1)) = v1
    return 0
}

fn main() {
    print("\e[1;35m--- JUNO CRYPTOGRAPHY ENGINE ---\e[0m")

    let block = alloc(16)
    let key = alloc(32)

    *block = 305419896
    *(ptr_add(block, 1)) = 2596069104

    *key = 0x01020304
    *(ptr_add(key, 1)) = 0x05060708
    *(ptr_add(key, 2)) = 0x090A0B0C
    *(ptr_add(key, 3)) = 0x0D0E0F00

    print("\e[34mPlaintext: \e[0m ")
    print(*block)
    print(*(ptr_add(block, 1)))

    print("\n\e[36m[ ENCRYPTING... ]\e[0m")
    tea_encrypt(block, key)
    print("\e[33mEncrypted: \e[0m ")
    print(*block)
    print(*(ptr_add(block, 1)))

    print("\n\e[32m[ DECRYPTING... ]\e[0m")
    tea_decrypt(block, key)
    print("\e[32mDecrypted: \e[0m ")
    print(*block)
    print(*(ptr_add(block, 1)))

    if (*block == 305419896 && *(ptr_add(block, 1)) == 2596069104) {
        print("\n\e[1;32mRESULT: SUCCESS!\e[0m")
    } else {
        print("\n\e[1;31mRESULT: ERROR!\e[0m")
    }

    free(block, 16)
    free(key, 32)
    return 0
}

ФАЙЛ: ./examples/echo_server.juno
========================================
fn main(): int {
    print("=== Echo Server ===")

    let sock = socket(2, 1, 0)
    print("Socket fd:")
    print(sock)

    if (sock < 0) {
        print("Socket failed!")
        return 1
    }

    let opt = 1

    let addr = ip(0, 0, 0, 0)
    let port = 9999
    print("Binding to port 9999...")

    let res = bind(sock, addr, port)
    print("Bind result:")
    print(res)

    if (res < 0) {
        print("Bind failed!")
        close(sock)
        return 1
    }

    listen(sock, 5)
    print("Listening...")

    print("Waiting for client...")
    let client = accept(sock)
    print("Client fd:")
    print(client)

    if (client >= 0) {
        print("Client connected!")

        let buf = getbuf()
        let running = 1

        while (running == 1) {
            let n = recv(client, buf, 1024)
            print("Received bytes:")
            print(n)

            if (n > 0) {
                send(client, buf, n)
            } else {
                running = 0
            }
        }

        close(client)
    }

    close(sock)
    print("Done")
    return 0
}

    print("y =")
    print(p.y)

    p.x = p.x + 5
    p.y = p.y - 3
    print("After move:")
    print("x =")
    print(p.x)
    print("y =")
    print(p.y)

    let rect = Rectangle
    rect.width = 10
    rect.height = 5

    print("Rectangle 10x5")

    let area = rect.width * rect.height

fn main(): int {
    prints("=== Juno StdLib Demo ===")

    prints("\n[Memory]")
    let ptr = malloc(1024)
    if (ptr != 0) {
        prints("Allocated 1KB")
        memset(ptr, 0, 1024)
        free(ptr)
        prints("Freed")
    }

    prints("\n[Strings]")

    let num = 12345
    let s = int_to_str(num)
    prints("int_to_str(12345):")
    prints(s)

    let str = "42"
    let n = str_to_int(str)
    prints("str_to_int(42):")
    print(n)

    let hello = "hello"
    prints("str_len(hello):")
    print(str_len(hello))

    prints("\n[Vector]")
    let v = vec_new(16)

    vec_push(v, 10)
    vec_push(v, 20)
    vec_push(v, 30)

    prints("Pushed 10, 20, 30")
    prints("vec_len:")
    print(vec_len(v))

    prints("vec_get(1):")
    print(vec_get(v, 1))

    let popped = vec_pop(v)
    prints("vec_pop:")
    print(popped)

    prints("\n[Files]")

    let fd = file_open("/tmp/juno_test.txt", 1)
    if (fd > 0) {
        file_writeln(fd, "Hello from Juno!")
        file_writeln(fd, "Line 2")
        file_close(fd)
        prints("Wrote /tmp/juno_test.txt")
    }

    if (file_exists("/tmp/juno_test.txt") == 1) {
        prints("File exists!")
        let content = file_read_all("/tmp/juno_test.txt")
        if (content != 0) {
            prints("Content:")
            prints(content)
        }
    }

    prints("\n=== Done ===")
    return 0
}

fn main() {
    output("--- JUNO PRIME FINDER (2-100) ---");

    let total_found = 0;

    for (n = 2; n <= 100; n++) {
        let is_prime = 1;

        for (i = 2; i < n; i++) {
            if (n % i == 0) {
                is_prime = 0;
            }
        }

        if (is_prime == 1) {
            output_int(n);
            total_found = total_found + 1;
        }
    }

    output("---------------------------------");
    output("Total Primes found:");
    output_int(total_found);

    return 0;
}

extern fn abs(n: i32) -> i32 from "libc.so.6"

    let val = -123
    let a = abs(val)
    print("abs(-123) is:")
    print(a)

    let s = "FFI is working!"
    let l = strlen(s)

fn main(): int {
    print("=== TCP Echo Server ===")

    let sock = socket(2, 1, 0)
    if (sock < 0) {
        print("Error: socket failed")
        return 1
    }
    print("Socket created")

    let addr = ip(0, 0, 0, 0)
    let result = bind(sock, addr, 12345)
    if (result < 0) {
        print("Error: bind failed")
        close(sock)
        return 1
    }
    print("Bound to port 12345")

    listen(sock, 5)
    print("Listening on port 12345...")

    let client = accept(sock)
    if (client < 0) {
        print("Error: accept failed")
        close(sock)
        return 1
    }
    print("Client connected!")

    let buf = getbuf()
    let running = 1

    while (running != 0) {
        let n = recv(client, buf, 1024)
        if (n <= 0) {
            running = 0
        } else {
            print("Received:")
            prints(buf)
            send(client, buf, n)
        }
    }

    close(client)
    close(sock)
    print("Server stopped")
    return 0
}

fn send_message(token: string, chat_id: string, text: string) {
    let url = concat("https://api.telegram.org/bot", token)
    let url2 = concat(url, "/sendMessage")

    let body1 = concat("{\"chat_id\":\"", chat_id)
    let body2 = concat(body1, "\",\"text\":\"")
    let body3 = concat(body2, text)
    let body = concat(body3, "\"}")

    let response = curl_post(url2, body)
    prints(response)
}

fn get_updates(token: string, offset: int): string {
    let url = concat("https://api.telegram.org/bot", token)
    let url2 = concat(url, "/getUpdates?timeout=30&offset=")

    let buf = getbuf()
    let url3 = concat(url2, "0")

    let response = curl_get(url3)
    return response
}

fn main(): int {
    let token = "YOUR_BOT_TOKEN"

    prints("Telegram Bot Started!")
    prints("Checking for updates...")

    let updates = get_updates(token, 0)
    prints("Updates:")
    prints(updates)

    return 0
}

fn main(): int {
    print("=== HTTP Client ===")

    let sock = socket(2, 1, 0)
    if (sock < 0) {
        print("Error: socket failed")
        return 1
    }
    print("Socket created:")
    print(sock)

    let addr = ip(127, 0, 0, 1)
    let result = connect(sock, addr, 8888)
    if (result < 0) {
        print("Error: connect failed (is server running on port 8080?)")
        close(sock)
        return 1
    }
    print("Connected to 127.0.0.1:8080")

    let request = "GET / HTTP/1.0\r\nHost: localhost\r\n\r\n"
    send(sock, request, 37)
    print("Request sent")

    let buf = getbuf()
    let received = recv(sock, buf, 4000)
    print("Received bytes:")
    print(received)

    if (received > 0) {
        print("Response:")
        prints(buf)
    }

    close(sock)
    print("Connection closed")
    return 0
}

fn main(): int {
    prints("=== memfd_create Demo ===")

    fd = memfd_create("juno_memfd", MFD_CLOEXEC())
    prints("Created memfd, fd:")
    print(fd)

    if (fd < 0) {
        prints("Error: memfd_create failed")
        return 1
    }

    msg = "Hello from memfd!"
    len = str_len(msg)
    written = write(fd, msg, len)
    prints("Bytes written:")
    print(written)

    lseek(fd, 0, 0)

    buf = malloc(64)
    bytes_read = read(fd, buf, 64)
    prints("Bytes read:")
    print(bytes_read)

    prints("Content:")
    prints(buf)

    free(buf)
    close(fd)

    prints("=== Done ===")
    return 0
}

fn main(): int {
    print("Array Demo")

    let numbers[5]
    numbers[0] = 10
    numbers[1] = 20
    numbers[2] = 30
    numbers[3] = 40
    numbers[4] = 50

    print("Array: [10, 20, 30, 40, 50]")

    let mut total = 0
    for (i = 0; i < 5; i++) {
        total = total + numbers[i]
    }
    print("Sum:")
    print(total)

    let mut max = numbers[0]
    for (i = 1; i < 5; i++) {
        if (numbers[i] > max) {
            max = numbers[i]
        }
    }
    print("Max:")
    print(max)

    let p = &numbers[0]
    print("First via pointer:")
    print(*p)

    let p2 = ptr_add(p, 2)
    print("Third via ptr_add:")
    print(*p2)

    return 0
}

fn main() {
    let host = trim(file_read_safe("/etc/hostname"))
    let kernel = trim(file_read_all("/proc/sys/kernel/osrelease"))

    let mut gui = "Server Mode"
    if (exists("/tmp/.X11-unix") == 1) {
        gui = "X11 Desktop"
    }

    let cyan = "\e[36m"
    let white = "\e[37m"
    let rst = "\e[0m"

    output("")
    let login = "root@"
    output("  " + cyan + "      _                      " + white + login + host)
    output("  " + cyan + "     | |                     " + rst + "-----------------")

    output("  " + cyan + "     | |_   _  _ __    ___   " + cyan + "OS:      " + rst + "Debian Trixie")

    let k_info = "Kernel:  " + kernel
    output("  " + cyan + " _   | | | | || '_ \\  / _ \\  " + cyan + k_info)

    output("  " + cyan + "| |__| | |_| || | | || (_) | " + cyan + "CPU:     " + rst + "AMD Ryzen 5")
    output("  " + cyan + " \\____/ \\__,_||_| |_| \\___/  " + cyan + "Memory:  " + rst + "16GB RAM")

    let gui_full = "GUI:     " + gui
    output("  " + cyan + "                             " + cyan + gui_full)

    output("  " + cyan + "                             " + cyan + "Lang:    " + rst + "Juno v3.0")

    output("")
    output("  " + "\e[40m   \e[41m   \e[42m   \e[43m   \e[44m   \e[45m   \e[46m   \e[47m   " + rst)
    output("")

    return 0
}

ФАЙЛ: ./examples/httpd.juno

#define PORT 8888
#define BACKLOG 10
#define BUF_SIZE 4096
#define VERSION 1

#ifdef LINUX
#define SERVER_NAME "MicroHTTPD/1.0 (Juno)"
#endif

#define HTTP_200 200
#define HTTP_404 404
#define HTTP_500 500

let g_requests = 0
let g_bytes_sent = 0

fn send_header(client: int, code: int, content_type: ptr, content_len: int): int {
    let buf = getbuf()

    if (code == HTTP_200) {
        let resp = "HTTP/1.0 200 OK\r\n"
        send(client, resp, 17)
    } else {
        if (code == HTTP_404) {
            let resp = "HTTP/1.0 404 Not Found\r\n"
            send(client, resp, 24)
        } else {
            let resp = "HTTP/1.0 500 Error\r\n"
            send(client, resp, 20)
        }
    }

    let ct = "Content-Type: text/html\r\n"
    send(client, ct, 25)

    let srv = "Server: MicroHTTPD/1.0\r\n"
    send(client, srv, 24)

    let conn = "Connection: close\r\n"
    send(client, conn, 19)

    let end = "\r\n"
    send(client, end, 2)

    return 0
}

fn send_html_page(client: int, title: ptr, body: ptr): int {
    let html1 = "<!DOCTYPE html><html><head><title>"
    send(client, html1, 34)

    send(client, title, len(title))

    let html2 = "</title><style>body{font-family:monospace;margin:40px;background:#1a1a2e;color:#eee}h1{color:#0f0}pre{background:#0d0d1a;padding:20px;border-radius:8px}</style></head><body>"
    send(client, html2, 167)

    send(client, body, len(body))

    let html3 = "</body></html>"
    send(client, html3, 14)

    return 0
}

fn handle_index(client: int): int {
    send_header(client, HTTP_200, "text/html", 0)

    let title = "MicroHTTPD"
    let body = "<h1>Welcome to MicroHTTPD</h1><p>A minimal HTTP server written in Juno.</p><h2>Endpoints:</h2><ul><li><a href='/'>/ - This page</a></li><li><a href='/status'>/status - Server status</a></li><li><a href='/info'>/info - System info</a></li><li><a href='/api'>/api - JSON API</a></li></ul><p><em>Powered by Juno v1.5</em></p>"

    send_html_page(client, title, body)
    return 0
}

fn handle_status(client: int): int {
    send_header(client, HTTP_200, "text/html", 0)

    let html = "<!DOCTYPE html><html><head><title>Status</title></head><body style='font-family:monospace;background:#1a1a2e;color:#eee;margin:40px'>"
    send(client, html, 131)

    let h1 = "<h1 style='color:#0f0'>Server Status</h1><pre>"
    send(client, h1, 46)

    let req = "Requests handled: "
    send(client, req, 18)

    let buf = getbuf()
    let count = g_requests

    if (count < 10) {
        let digit = count + 48
        memset(buf, digit, 1)
        memset(ptr_add(buf, 1), 0, 1)
    } else {
        memset(buf, 48 + (count / 10), 1)
        memset(ptr_add(buf, 1), 48 + (count - (count / 10) * 10), 1)
        memset(ptr_add(buf, 2), 0, 1)
    }
    send(client, buf, 2)

    let nl = "\nServer PID: "
    send(client, nl, 12)

    let pid = getpid()
    if (pid < 10000) {
        let d1 = pid / 1000
        let d2 = (pid / 100) - d1 * 10
        let d3 = (pid / 10) - (pid / 100) * 10
        let d4 = pid - (pid / 10) * 10
        memset(buf, 48 + d1, 1)
        memset(ptr_add(buf, 1), 48 + d2, 1)
        memset(ptr_add(buf, 2), 48 + d3, 1)
        memset(ptr_add(buf, 3), 48 + d4, 1)
        send(client, buf, 4)
    }

    let end = "\nStatus: Running</pre></body></html>"
    send(client, end, 37)

    return 0
}

fn handle_info(client: int): int {
    send_header(client, HTTP_200, "text/html", 0)

    let title = "System Info"

    let pid = getpid()
    let uid = getuid()

    let body = "<h1>System Information</h1><pre>Platform: Linux x86_64\nCompiler: Juno v1.5\nFeatures:\n  - Native x64 codegen\n  - Preprocessor\n  - Sized types (i8-u64)\n  - Bitwise ops\n  - Pointer arithmetic\n  - System calls\n  - Atomic operations\n  - Network sockets</pre>"

    send_html_page(client, title, body)
    return 0
}

fn handle_api(client: int): int {
    let header = "HTTP/1.0 200 OK\r\nContent-Type: application/json\r\nServer: MicroHTTPD/1.0\r\nConnection: close\r\n\r\n"
    send(client, header, 91)

    let json = "{server:MicroHTTPD,version:1.0,language:Juno,status:running}"
    send(client, json, 59)

    return 0
}

fn handle_404(client: int): int {
    send_header(client, HTTP_404, "text/html", 0)

    let title = "404 Not Found"
    let body = "<h1 style='color:red'>404 - Not Found</h1><p>The requested page was not found.</p><p><a href='/'>Go to homepage</a></p>"

    send_html_page(client, title, body)
    return 0
}

fn handle_request(client: int, request: ptr): int {

    let ptr4 = ptr_add(request, 4)
    let c4 = u8(*ptr4)

    if (c4 == 47) {
        let ptr5 = ptr_add(request, 5)
        let c5 = u8(*ptr5)

        if (c5 == 32) {
            return handle_index(client)
        }
        if (c5 == 115) {
            return handle_status(client)
        }
        if (c5 == 105) {
            return handle_info(client)
        }
        if (c5 == 97) {
            return handle_api(client)
        }
    }

    return handle_404(client)
}

fn handle_client(client: int): int {
    let buf = getbuf()

    let n = recv(client, buf, BUF_SIZE)

    if (n > 0) {
        g_requests++
        handle_request(client, buf)
    }

    close(client)
    return 0
}

fn server_loop(sock: int): int {
    print("Waiting for connections...")

    let max_requests = 5
    let handled = 0

    while (handled < max_requests) {
        let client = accept(sock)

        if (client >= 0) {
            print("Client connected!")
            handle_client(client)
            handled++
            print("Request handled")
        }
    }

    print("Max requests reached, shutting down")
    return 0
}

fn main(): int {
    print("========================================")
    print("  MicroHTTPD - Juno HTTP Server")
    print("  Port: 8888")
    print("========================================")

    let sock = socket(2, 1, 0)
    if (sock < 0) {
        print("ERROR: Cannot create socket")
        return 1
    }
    print("Socket created")

    let addr = ip(0, 0, 0, 0)
    let result = bind(sock, addr, PORT)
    if (result < 0) {
        print("ERROR: Cannot bind to port 8888")
        close(sock)
        return 1
    }
    print("Bound to port 8888")

    listen(sock, BACKLOG)
    print("Listening...")
    print("")
    print("Open in browser: http://localhost:8888")
    print("")

    server_loop(sock)

    close(sock)
    return 0
}

import "../stdlib/std.juno"

fn main() {
    prints("Testing Epoll support...\n")

    let l_obj[1]
    let loop: EpollLoop = &l_obj[0]
    loop.init()

    if loop.epfd < 0 {
        prints("Failed to create epoll instance\n")
        return 1
    }

    prints("Epoll FD: ")
    print(loop.epfd)
    prints("\n")

    let res = loop.add(0, epoll_in())
    if res < 0 {
        prints("Failed to add stdin to epoll\n")
    } else {
        prints("Successfully added stdin to epoll loop\n")
    }

    prints("Wait for event (timeout 1s)... ")
    let events[10]
    res = loop.wait(&events[0], 5, 1000)

    if res == 0 {
        prints("Timeout (as expected if you didn't type anything)\n")
    } else {
        if res > 0 {
            prints("Got event!\n")
        } else {
            prints("Error in epoll_wait\n")
        }
    }

    prints("Demo finished.\n")
    return 0
}

========================================
ФАЙЛ: ./examples/minishell.juno
========================================
#define MAX_INPUT 256
#define MAX_ARGS 16
#define VERSION 1

#ifdef LINUX
#define SHELL_PROMPT "jsh> "
#endif

struct HistoryEntry {
    cmd: ptr
    next: ptr
}

let g_running = 1
let g_history_head = 0
let g_history_count = 0
let g_last_exit_code = 0

fn builtin_exit(args: ptr): int {
    print("Goodbye!")
    g_running = 0
    return 0
}

fn builtin_help(args: ptr): int {
    print("MiniShell v1.0 - Built-in commands:")
    print("  help     - Show this help")
    print("  exit     - Exit shell")
    print("  pwd      - Print working directory")
    print("  cd DIR   - Change directory")
    print("  pid      - Show shell PID")
    print("  history  - Show command history")
    print("  clear    - Clear screen")
    print("  status   - Show last exit code")
    print("  mem      - Memory info")
    print("  env      - Show environment")
    return 0
}

fn builtin_pwd(args: ptr): int {
    let buf = getbuf()
    getcwd(buf, 1024)
    prints(buf)
    return 0
}

fn builtin_cd(args: ptr): int {
    let result = chdir("/tmp")
    if (result < 0) {
        print("cd: failed")
        return 1
    }
    return 0
}

fn builtin_pid(args: ptr): int {
    let pid = getpid()
    let uid = getuid()
    print("Shell PID:")
    print(pid)
    print("User ID:")
    print(uid)
    return 0
}

fn builtin_history(args: ptr): int {
    print("Command history:")
    print(g_history_count)
    return 0
}

fn builtin_clear(args: ptr): int {
    print("\x1b[2J\x1b[H")
    return 0
}

fn builtin_status(args: ptr): int {
    print("Last exit code:")
    print(g_last_exit_code)
    return 0
}

fn builtin_mem(args: ptr): int {
    print("=== Memory Info ===")

    let prot = PROT_READ() | PROT_WRITE()
    let flags = MAP_PRIVATE() | MAP_ANONYMOUS()
    let mem = mmap(0, 4096, prot, flags, 0, 0)

    if (mem != 0) {
        print("Test allocation: OK")
        print("Address:")
        print(mem)
        munmap(mem, 4096)
        print("Freed: OK")
    } else {
        print("Allocation failed!")
    }

    return 0
}

fn builtin_env(args: ptr): int {
    print("=== Environment ===")
    print("Shell: MiniShell v1.0")
    print("Platform: Linux x86_64")
    print("Compiler: Juno v1.5")

    let pid = getpid()
    print("PID:")
    print(pid)

    let buf = getbuf()
    getcwd(buf, 1024)
    print("CWD:")
    prints(buf)

    return 0
}

fn try_builtin(cmd: ptr): int {
    let c0 = *cmd

    if (c0 == 101) {
        return builtin_exit(cmd)
    }

    if (c0 == 104) {
        return builtin_help(cmd)
    }

    if (c0 == 112) {
        let c1 = *(ptr_add(cmd, 0))
        let ptr1 = ptr_add(cmd, 1)
        let c1_val = u8(*ptr1)
        if (c1_val == 119) {
            return builtin_pwd(cmd)
        }
        if (c1_val == 105) {
            return builtin_pid(cmd)
        }
    }

    if (c0 == 99) {
        let ptr1 = ptr_add(cmd, 1)
        let c1 = u8(*ptr1)
        if (c1 == 100) {
            return builtin_cd(cmd)
        }
        if (c1 == 108) {
            return builtin_clear(cmd)
        }
    }

    if (c0 == 115) {
        return builtin_status(cmd)
    }

    if (c0 == 109) {
        return builtin_mem(cmd)
    }

    if (c0 == 101) {
        let ptr1 = ptr_add(cmd, 1)
        let c1 = u8(*ptr1)
        if (c1 == 110) {
            return builtin_env(cmd)
        }
    }

    return 0 - 1
}

fn execute_external(cmd: ptr): int {
    print("External command not implemented yet")
    print("Use built-in commands: help, exit, pwd, cd, pid, mem, env, status, clear")
    return 127
}

fn process_command(input: ptr): int {
    let first = u8(*input)
    if (first == 0) {
        return 0
    }
    if (first == 10) {
        return 0
    }

    g_history_count++

    let result = try_builtin(input)
    if (result != 0 - 1) {
        g_last_exit_code = result
        return result
    }

    result = execute_external(input)
    g_last_exit_code = result
    return result
}

fn show_prompt(): int {
    print("jsh> ")
    return 0
}

fn shell_loop(): int {
    let input_buf = getbuf()

    while (g_running != 0) {
        show_prompt()

        let n = read(0, input_buf, MAX_INPUT)

        if (n <= 0) {
            print("")
            g_running = 0
        } else {
            process_command(input_buf)
        }
    }

    return g_last_exit_code
}

fn main(): int {
    print("=====================================")
    print("  MiniShell v1.0 - Juno Shell")
    print("  Type 'help' for commands")
    print("=====================================")

    let pid = getpid()
    print("Shell started with PID:")
    print(pid)
    print("")

    let exit_code = shell_loop()

    print("Shell exited with code:")
    print(exit_code)

    return exit_code
}
-e
